[1]English
<h2>Ryan Eakins&rsquo;s <em>Coelacanth Quartet</em></h2>
The <em>Coelacanth Quartet</em> details the adventures of Corla, a Tsarin telepath far from home. In the first book, she finds herself in Zhalad, and soon discovers a plot to take over that realm. Here is that first tale, provisionally titled&hellip;
&date=20170716
[2]The Crackled Egg
The <em>Crackled Egg</em> takes place in Zhalad. Two races of people live there. While two Zhaladi or two Fezhel can easily telepathically receive and project emotion amongst themselves, a Zhaladi encountering a Fezhel has no such ability. Thus the two races tend to live separately.
Vedran, advisor to a weak ruler, hears of a device capable of increasing one&rsquo;s emotional projection abilities to such a degree that one could lead a country&rsquo;s people by their hearts. He attempts to track down this device, with the hope of displacing his king.
&date=20170716
[3]Prelude
<span class="version-anchor" id="0"></span>Corla came back to consciousness slowly, the heat and the coarseness of the sand on which she sat penetrating her mind. She gingerly stood up. Her legs ached from holding the meditative pose for so long.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#0">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#0">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#0">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#0">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="1"></span><em>One down, two to go,</em> she thought to herself. <em>By the Six gods of Tinellb, I&rsquo;ll be glad to finish this and have some peace.</em> She allowed herself to feel grief for a moment, grief at being continually separated from her beloved.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#1">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#1">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#1">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#1">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="2"></span>Realising that activity was the surest way to finding him again, she stood up to take stock of her situation. Underneath the thin layer of sand, she could feel paving stones. Only natural sounds could be heard, and the sense of human life was far distant.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#2">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#2">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#2">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#2">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="3"></span><em>A road perhaps. At least, I hope so.</em> The sun could be felt over her left shoulder. <em>Is it sunrise or sunset? Am I facing east or west?</em><span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#3">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#3">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#3">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#3">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="4"></span>The strongest sense of life was opposite the sun. She couldn&rsquo;t tell how far, but she realised that nothing was going to be solved by sitting still.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#4">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#4">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#4">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#4">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="5"></span>She unfolded her walking stick and carefully began inventing time-travel.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#5">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#5">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#5">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#5">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="6"></span><span class="stars">*&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*</span><span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#6">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#6">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#6">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#6">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="7"></span>Market week! Toresh&rsquo;s heart sang within her. That glorious time to take goods down to the flatlands, trading olives and goat cheese for wheat flour and papyrus. A chance to meet exotic people and get away from the hillfolk for a time. A chance to exchange the familiar smells of goat and heath for the scent of the silty river.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#7">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#7">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#7">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#7">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="8"></span>She finished helping her parents fill the wagon. She had helped in the goat pens since she learned to walk, but only been allowed to travel down the hills within the last few years.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#8">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#8">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#8">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#8">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="9"></span>Piado felt his daughter&rsquo;s excitement from across the compound. He reached out with his own heart, sending the pride he felt for her. He farewelled the village elder, and his own wife, and walked across to join Toresh and the wagon.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#9">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#9">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#9">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#9">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="10"></span>With a slight touch of the reins to the back of the draughtsbeast, the wagon started moving. Piado was driving for the first leg of the journey, following the river gorge down the hills. The river could be seen far below, little more than a trickle at this time of year. Toresh&rsquo;s initial excitement faded as she was lulled into sleep by the gently rocking wagon. Piado encouraged her sleepiness because he knew he would need her awake if they were to best the flatlanders.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#10">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#10">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#10">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#10">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="11"></span>There was no one on the road. The only sounds were those made by the wagon and the draughtsbeast.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#11">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#11">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#11">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#11">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="12"></span>As the wagon came around a corner, Piado checked the draughtsbeast&rsquo;s movement just in time to avoid a short figure. He started yelling at her to move, but stopped when she raised sightless eyes to him.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#12">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#12">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#12">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#12">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="13"></span>&ldquo;I&rsquo;m sorry for yelling at you, but what are you doing out here by yourself? Are you lost?&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#13">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#13">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#13">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#13">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="14"></span>Words in an alien language were his only reply. Handing the reins to his suddenly very alert daughter, he got out of the wagon. He had assumed her to be a flatlander since he couldn&rsquo;t sense her emotions, but realised otherwise when he noticed the paleness of her skin. He reached out for her hand, placed it on his chest, and said his own name. Moving her hand back to her, he learned her name.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#14">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#14">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#14">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#14">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="15"></span>&ldquo;Corla.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#15">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#15">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#15">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#15">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="16"></span>Piado led the woman over to the wagon and introduced her to Toresh. He motioned to his daughter to move across to allow Corla to ascend.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#16">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#16">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#16">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#16">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="17"></span><span class="stars">*&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*</span><span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#17">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#17">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#17">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#17">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="18"></span>Within only a few hours in this world, Corla had found herself firmly ensconced between the two farmers. The rest of the day was spent travelling. She dozed in her seat, letting their conversation pass through her.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#18">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#18">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#18">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#18">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="19"></span>As night fell, Piado chose a place beside the road to rest. Dinner was a spiced lentil stew, prepared by Toresh. Piado gave his tent up to the stranger, and slept in the wagon covered with the tarp.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#19">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#19">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#19">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#19">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="20"></span>The ground was chill the next morning, but the bright sun soon evaporated the frost and warmed the air.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#20">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#20">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#20">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#20">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="21"></span>The wagon reached the market town of Lusov early in the afternoon. Piado stayed with Corla and the wagon as Toresh sought out the market authorities to reserve her place in the bazaar.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#21">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#21">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#21">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#21">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="22"></span>&ldquo;Piado, I wanted to thank you for everything you&rsquo;ve done for me.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#22">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#22">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#22">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#22">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="23"></span>Piado let out a startled exclamation. &ldquo;I thought you couldn&rsquo;t speak! Why didn&rsquo;t you say something before?&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#23">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#23">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#23">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#23">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="24"></span>&ldquo;It took me some time to learn your language. I&rsquo;m not an empath the way your people are, I&rsquo;m a telepath.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#24">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#24">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#24">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#24">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="25"></span>&ldquo;Our people? Where are you from?&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#25">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#25">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#25">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#25">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="26"></span>&ldquo;This may be a little difficult to explain. Do you know anything about your history? Your ultimate history, perhaps?&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#26">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#26">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#26">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#26">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="27"></span>&ldquo;A telepath? What am I thinking right now, then?&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#27">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#27">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#27">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#27">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="28"></span>&ldquo;My abilities only seem to work properly on my own people,&rdquo; Corla replied. &ldquo;I can pick up enough to tell me where population centres are, and apparently to pick up your language, but that is it.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#28">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#28">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#28">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#28">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="29"></span>Piado rolled his eyes in disbelief. He swung his legs out over the side of the cart, grunting as his did so. Once he was on the ground, he grasped Corla&rsquo;s hand and helped her off.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#29">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#29">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#29">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#29">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="30"></span>He led her to a two-storey stone building on the main street of Lusov. A quick scan of the building&rsquo;s manifest told him where he was going. In a room at the end of the corridor, they found a woman sitting behind a desk. She was wearing the officious robes that the flatlanders wore for formal occasions. Piado explained his side of the story, but before Corla had a chance to speak, the bureaucrat rang a small bell. Her assistant appeared from a side door.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#30">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#30">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#30">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#30">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="31"></span>&ldquo;Is Tepeth awoken from her nap yet?&rdquo; she was asked.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#31">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#31">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#31">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#31">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="32"></span>The assistant nodded, and then left the room at a gesture from the official.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#32">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#32">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#32">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#32">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="33"></span>&ldquo;Her Honour will take care of this,&rdquo; Piado was informed. &ldquo;Kolina, is it? Come with me.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#33">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#33">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#33">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#33">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="34"></span>Piado attempted to follow, but was prevented from doing so by the closing of the door behind the departing pair. He forgot each time he was among his own people how rude these were. Realising there was nothing further to do, he went back to the draughtsbeast and his waiting daughter.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#34">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#34">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#34">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#34">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="35"></span><span class="stars">*&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*</span><span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#35">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#35">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#35">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#35">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="36"></span>Corla was pushed along the passageway, trying not to trip on anything. She heard a door being opened ahead of her and could tell from the echoes around that she was now in a small room. The official unceremoniously led her to a bench, sat her down, and then left again.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#36">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#36">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#36">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#36">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="37"></span>Alone in the room, Corla got up and felt her way around the wall. She opened both doors, one at a time, but no one answered her calls. Standing at a tall window, she could smell the city and feel the noonday sun upon her face.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#37">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#37">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#37">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#37">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="38"></span>She was just about to try the doors again when one was opened from the outside.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#38">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#38">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#38">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#38">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="39"></span>The assistant&rsquo;s voice said something in her own language, and Corla told her in Piado&rsquo;s tongue that she could not understand her.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#39">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#39">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#39">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#39">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="40"></span>&ldquo;Oh, so you only speak Fezhel, do you?&rdquo; she said, switching to that. &ldquo;I just asked if you were hungry. You&rsquo;re lucky to have me; I&rsquo;m the only one around here who bothered to learn from our northern neighbours. You don&rsquo;t look like a Topper, I beg your pardon, like a Toplander. Were you not told about the food there on the counter?&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#40">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#40">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#40">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#40">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="41"></span>Taken aback by the sudden stream of words, Corla could only shake her head.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#41">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#41">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#41">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#41">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="42"></span>&ldquo;People around here! So inconsiderate! Like she expects a blind person to just know that there&rsquo;s food here. On behalf of the Council, I apologise. Anyway, my name is Lharen. Besi said you were Kolina?&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#42">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#42">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#42">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#42">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="43"></span>She corrected her, and then said that she was actually hungry.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#43">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#43">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#43">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#43">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="44"></span>&ldquo;Where have my manners gone now? I&rsquo;m just as bad as they are, assuming that you&rsquo;ll just find the food on my say-so. Corla? That&rsquo;s an unusual name.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#44">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#44">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#44">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#44">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="45"></span>Corla smiled in her direction and she came up and took her over to the counter, where indeed sat a box of biscuits and a store of warm water. Lharen put something she could smell into a cup of the water, and she gathered her thoughts to explain her story.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#45">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#45">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#45">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#45">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="46"></span><span class="stars">*&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;*</span><span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#46">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#46">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#46">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#46">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="47"></span>While waiting for her father to return, Toresh sought out their usual sleeping place &mdash; a small hotel on the corner. Piado entered the room just as she had finished putting their gear away.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#47">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#47">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#47">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#47">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="48"></span>&ldquo;Hey, kiddo. Are you hungry?&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#48">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#48">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#48">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#48">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="49"></span>&ldquo;A little, father,&rdquo; Toresh replied. &ldquo;Is Corla alright?&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#49">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#49">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#49">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#49">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="50"></span>&ldquo;I hope so, but it seems that she&rsquo;s their problem now.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#50">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#50">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#50">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#50">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="51"></span>Piado put his arm around his daughter&rsquo;s shoulder and walked her out the door. In the hotel restaurant, they ordered something cheap to eat. They knew that tomorrow should bring them more money, and that the next time they dined, they would be able to have something tastier.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#51">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#51">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#51">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#51">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="52"></span>The next day dawned bright and hot. The haze came up as usual around the large town of Lusov. Piado and Toresh hurried out of their hotel room and into the market, carrying their wares. Piado stood behind their set-up table, while Toresh put on her most winning smile, trying to get the busy townspeople to try their produce. The trading progressed throughout the morning. Lusov usually became too hot around noon, so the town usually went to siesta.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#52">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#52">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#52">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#52">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="53"></span>The sun was just beginning to set when Lharen came by, guiding Corla by her side. The assistant was clearly not here to buy anything.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#53">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#53">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#53">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#53">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="54"></span>&ldquo;What are you two doing here?&rdquo; Piado asked, astonished.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#54">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#54">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#54">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#54">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="55"></span>&ldquo;It&rsquo;s her idea, sir,&rdquo; Lharen answered. &ldquo;She&rsquo;s got this idea that meeting you was fated or something.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#55">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#55">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#55">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#55">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="56"></span>&ldquo;It&rsquo;s not fate,&rdquo; Corla corrected her. &ldquo;I just know that what I need to do here, on Zhalad, is something to do with you.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#56">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#56">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#56">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#56">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="57"></span>&ldquo;What?&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#57">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#57">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#57">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#57">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="58"></span>&ldquo;I&rsquo;m trying to get home. Every other place I&rsquo;ve been, it seems that I need to complete some task. I have the strongest feeling that you&rsquo;re involved.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#58">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#58">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#58">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#58">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="59"></span>&ldquo;What do you want us to do about it?&rdquo; Piado seemed uninterested.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#59">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#59">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#59">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#59">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="60"></span>&ldquo;Take me with you. I am not afraid of work.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#60">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#60">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#60">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#60">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="61"></span>&ldquo;With all due respect, you&rsquo;re blind. What use could you be to us? I did my charity by bringing you here. Now, I&rsquo;m done.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#61">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#61">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#61">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#61">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="62"></span>Toresh could feel his temper growing. She tugged at his sleeve. &ldquo;Please, father, calm yourself. I&rsquo;m sure we can find something for her to do. It&rsquo;s not that difficult to talk to customers.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#62">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#62">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#62">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#62">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="63"></span>Corla spoke up. &ldquo;I do actually have customer experience. I may even have a slight advantage; you can&rsquo;t sense flatlander emotions. I can. Well, at least, my abilities should be able to pick up something.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#63">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#63">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#63">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#63">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="64"></span>Piado capitulated. &ldquo;Fine. Make yourself useful and you can stay with us. The village council can decide what to do with you when we get home.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#64">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#64">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#64">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#64">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="65"></span>Lharen guided Corla behind the market table, and then took her leave.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#65">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#65">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#65">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#65">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="67"></span>The market was clearly closing, so Toresh and her father went back to the hotel, taking Corla with them. Corla used some money she had gained from Lharen to pay for her own dinner, and found herself in the bunkhouse, where she had to share lodgings with a few other people.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#67">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#67">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#67">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#67">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>&date=20170807
<span class="version-anchor" id="67"></span>Toresh came around the next morning to take her to breakfast, and thence to her first day in the Lusov markets.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#67">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#67">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#67">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#67">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="68"></span>As she had hoped, Corla got enough impressions from the swirling thoughts around her to be able to predict which customers could be persuaded to part with more currency, and which would be happier to barter. Even Piado was impressed, although only his daughter could tell; he did not let it show in his voice. Slowly through the day, their stores diminished as they were bought or traded for. The market went on for a couple of days yet, but Piado figured that tomorrow would see them finished. He was glad; he didn&rsquo;t mind the flatlanders on occasion, but it was very easy to become tired of them. He always needed to concentrate more, trying to communicate in words. <em>Still,</em> he reflected, <em>Corla seems to be doing what she promised. That does make it slightly easier.</em><span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#68">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#68">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#68">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#68">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="69"></span>Later that evening, when Piado had gone to bed, the two women remained awake, sipping their drinks in the bar. Toresh noticed Lharen standing in the doorway, and motioned her over.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#69">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#69">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#69">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#69">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>&date=20170808
<span class="version-anchor" id="70"></span>&ldquo;I hope you don&rsquo;t mind, Corla, but I invited Lharen out tonight. I don&rsquo;t get to interact with flatlanders much.&rdquo; She added an afterthought. &ldquo;Unless I&rsquo;m selling them something, of course.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#70">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#70">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#70">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#70">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="71"></span>&ldquo;No, that&rsquo;s fine. As long as she makes herself useful.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#71">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#71">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#71">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#71">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="72"></span>Lharen heard this as she neared the table. &ldquo;Ha. I get it. Next round is on me, right? I don&rsquo;t get out much, but I know how the game is played.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#72">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#72">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#72">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#72">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="73"></span>&ldquo;Don&rsquo;t get out much? Surely your job means you get to meet a lot of people,&rdquo; Toresh said.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#73">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#73">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#73">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#73">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="74"></span>&ldquo;Weren&rsquo;t you just making the same complaint?&rdquo; asked Corla.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#74">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#74">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#74">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#74">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="75"></span>&ldquo;While I do meet people, but I&rsquo;m just a service, really. They come in when they need something signed officially, or whatever. Never had a visitor from another world, though.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#75">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#75">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#75">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#75">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="76"></span>&ldquo;Speaking of which, what is that about, Corla?&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#76">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#76">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#76">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#76">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="77"></span>&ldquo;I&rsquo;m actually surprised that you&rsquo;re surprised, Toresh. After all, that has to be how both your people and Lharen&rsquo;s got here.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#77">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#77">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#77">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#77">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="78"></span>&ldquo;I&rsquo;m ashamed to admit that we didn&rsquo;t treat our subject peoples well.&rdquo; Lharen suddenly looked stricken. &rdquo;My greatest apologies, that&rsquo;s just how it&rsquo;s written in our histories. When the Fezhel came here, they lived under our rule. Part of what we did was to control their present by taking away their past. It&rsquo;s only in the last few generations that they were even allowed to speak their own language in public. In fact, until then, we were quite sure that no one spoke it at all anymore.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#78">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#78">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#78">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#78">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="79"></span>&ldquo;My grandfather told me of those times. As much as he had learned, anyway. There were always secrets being passed around, but I have never heard of anything like Corla is talking about.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#79">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#79">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#79">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#79">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="80"></span>Corla thought back to everything she had learned on the last world she had visited. &ldquo;I learned much of this on Brequ&eacute;, whence I most recently came. On my own world of Solaji, most of this is lost, too. All our peoples originally started on one world, but war tore us apart. A weapon was created that broke space-time, casting our cousins both to this world, and another similar. Lharen&rsquo;s people, and mine, are descended from that second group. I can only assume that when the Zhaladi came here, they were able to take control of this land from the original Fezhel.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#80">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#80">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#80">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#80">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="81"></span>Lharen nodded. &ldquo;That&rsquo;s my understanding, also. We have remnants of tools my ancestors used, but we&rsquo;re unable to recreate any of them. We can&rsquo;t even recognise most of the materials. In hiding the Fezhel&rsquo;s past, we seem to have lost our own, as well.&rdquo;<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#81">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#81">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#81">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#81">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="82"></span>A somber mood fell over the table.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#82">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#82">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#82">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#82">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="83"></span><span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#83">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#83">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#83">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#83">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>
<span class="version-anchor" id="84"></span>&date=20170807<span class="version-links"><a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#84">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#84">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#84">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#84">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>[3]Waterfall

This and subsequent pages are in Tinellbian script, beginning with the <a href="http://grammar.tinellb.com/highlulani/index.html">High Lulani</a> language. If you have trouble reading this, you may choose one another of the options to the left.

<h2>Daxunikifigi Qasa&rsquo;i Sinnanuruqa Ra&rsquo;aniqa &#x294;ikinnisa</h2>
This set of pages uses Latin letters to give an idea of the sounds of the Tinellbian languages.

[2]Xucipura Cula

[3]Disinnamuka
<span class="version-anchor" id="0"></span>Kurila cani pamilami matta naru, &rsquo;ala qira&rsquo;ataqa nigup&middot;ipi jagaru pamana. Cani janniditiba bataniqqi. Kanu ra&rsquo;u kal&middot;uli nicurilluru gupikarafi pi bi&rsquo;u.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../english/thecrackledegg/prelude.html#0">English</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#0">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#0">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#0">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>

<span class="version-anchor" id="7"></span>Kassurula musaqapi! &#x294;iluqa Turassi xisa&rsquo;i. <span class="version-anchor" id="10"></span>Sara cani kukipuqa rali sisa pada, &rsquo;ita&rsquo;&middot;i&rsquo;assa ra&rsquo;usi janni. Pi&rsquo;adu kikabijaju curriqa faluki janni&rsquo;ita&rsquo;ikka, jafa&rsquo;akaqa quhha qanulli janni. Quhha qa xidu &rsquo;usixa, pa ra&rsquo;u nifa&rsquo;idaqa laru suxudiini kituci. Qali&#x294;i mallijuakuqa Turassi tuhi cani, haru lanu kalu&rsquo;ita&rsquo;iqa janni&rsquo;issaru nara. Pi&rsquo;adu qirisunarakka quhu dumi daru&rsquo;i, li nirasi kalupamilamirudisi kissa&rsquo;agudanna nubitu&rsquo;afuri da&rsquo;aru lanu pagi.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../english/thecrackledegg/prelude.html#10">English</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#10">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../interlinear/story/prologue.html#10">Interlinear</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#10">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span>

[3]Prologue
[t]<span class="version-anchor" id="0"></span>Corla came back to consciousness slowly, the heat and the coarseness of the sand on which she sat penetrating her mind. She gingerly stood up. Her legs ached from holding the meditative pose for so long.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../english/thecrackledegg/prelude.html#0">English</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#0">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#0">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#0">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span> | [r]<div class="literal">Q&#x14d;la is becoming slowly conscious again, realising the heat and roughness of the sand in which (she) is sitting. (She) stands up carefully. (Her) legs are hurting because of sitting enlightened while time passed.</div> | [r]<div class="flex">[t]Kurila | [r]<ipa>CT:/&#x2c8;&#x1c2;&#x2b0;&#x254;&#x2d0;.l&#x259;/</ipa> | [/t][t]cani | [r]<small-caps>prs;dyn</small-caps> | [/t][t]pa- | milami | [r]think- | surroundings | [/t][t]matta | [r]again | [/t][t]naru, | [r]slowly, | [/t][t]&rsquo;ala | [r]heat | [/t][t]qira- | &rsquo;a- | ta- | qa | [r]rough- | <small-caps>nmn</small-caps>- | and- | <small-caps>gen</small-caps> | [/t][t]ni- | gup(i)- | pi | [r]in- | sit- | <small-caps>pst;sta</small-caps> | [/t][t]jagaru | [r]sand | [/t][t]pa- | mana. | [r]think- | realisation. | [/t][t]Cani | [r]<small-caps>prs;dyn</small-caps> | [/t][t]janni- | di- | tiba | [r]move- | up- | legs | [/t][t]bata- | niqqi. | [r]care- | <small-caps>qal</small-caps>. | [/t][t]Kanu | [r]Leg | [/t][t]ra&rsquo;u | [r]<small-caps>prs;sta</small-caps> | [/t][t]kal(u)- | li | [r]<small-caps>abl</small-caps>- | <small-caps>com</small-caps> | [/t][t]ni- | cur- | illu- | ru | [r]in- | time_passes- | <small-caps>psv</small-caps>- | <small-caps>ger</small-caps> | [/t][t]gupi- | karafi | [r]sit- | enlightenment | [/t][t]pi | [r]<small-caps>pst;sta</small-caps> | [/t][t]bi&rsquo;u. | [r]hurt. | [/t]</div>[/t]

[t]<span class="version-anchor" id="2"></span>Realising that activity was the surest way to finding him again, she stood up to take stock of her situation. Underneath the thin layer of sand, she could feel paving stones. Only natural sounds could be heard, and the sense of human life was far distant.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../english/thecrackledegg/prelude.html#2">English</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#2">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#2">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#2">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span> | [r]<div class="literal">Because (she) realises (the fact that) doing something is the strongest rope to hang his finding on, (she) stands up, (she) assesses her surroundings. [t]<span class="version-anchor" id="3"></span><em>A road perhaps. At least, I hope so.</em> The sun could be felt over her left shoulder. <em>Is it sunrise or sunset? [t]<span class="version-anchor" id="10"></span>With a slight touch of the reins to the back of the draughtsbeast, the wagon started moving. [t]<span class="version-anchor" id="52"></span>The next day dawned bright and hot. The haze came up as usual around the large town of Lusov. Piado and Toresh hurried out of their hotel room and into the market, carrying their wares. Piado stood behind their set-up table, while Toresh put on her most winning smile, trying to get the busy townspeople to try their produce. The trading progressed throughout the morning. Lusov usually became too hot around noon, so the town usually went to siesta.<span class="version-links"><a href="../../english/thecrackledegg/prelude.html#52">English</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../tinellbian/zcoryl/dsnuk.html#52">Tinellbian</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../transliteration/xucipuracula/disinnamuka.html#52">Transliteration</a>&nbsp;<a href="../../gloss/feather-becomingegg/up-story-nmn.html#52">Gloss</a>&nbsp;</span> | [r]<div class="literal">To the morning was heat and a bright light tomorrow. [t]<span class="version-anchor" id="70"></span> | [r][t] | [r] | [/t][/t]&date=20170808[1]Gloss
<h2>Three-tail-having Fish-called Story-four-<small-caps>gen</small-caps> Ryan-<small-caps>gen</small-caps> Eakins.</h2>
A &ldquo;threetail-having fish&rdquo; is a coelacanth, referring to the three lobes on the tail of members of this species. A &ldquo;feather-becoming egg&rdquo; is a rough translation of <em>crackled egg</em>, and refers to a hatchling emerging into the world.
